<title>[WUS-959] R-ASR075 and R-ASR077 Issue</title>
<link>http://helpdesk.hk.ncs-i.com/browse/WUS-959</link>
<description>
1. For R-ASR075-C and R-ASR075-E, when a single assessment/term or multiple assessments/terms are selected, the word &quot;總分&quot; and &quot;Total&quot; should not be included in the field heading of any subject components in the 1st page of the output files in PDF, WORD, RICHTEXT, EXCEL format and in the 1st sheet of the output file in EXCEL format (Print Excel in one-line per record). An example of the problem is shown in the dump screen below <br/> <br/> 2. For R-ASR077-C and R-ASR077-E, when multiple assessments/terms are selected, there are various discrepancies between the output files in PDF format and in EXCEL format (Print Excel in one-line per record). An example of the problem is shown in the dump screen below.
</description>

Subject component list is still written in English even in Chinese version. (Fig. 5) <br/> 7.	Please delete extra ＂ in Cat B result (Chinese Version) as shown in Fig. 6

<item>
<title>[WUS-938] R-ATT009 Problem</title>
<link>http://helpdesk.hk.ncs-i.com/browse/WUS-938</link>
<description>
For R-ATT009, <br/> <br/> 1. The student transferred from 1A to 1B in the middle of the school year. However, the record is duplicated in both classes. The display logic should tally with the current report (other formats such as PDF or original excel format) <br/> <br/> 2. The wait time for printing R-ATT009 is quite slow, can it be optimised? <br/>
</description>
<environment/>

<title>
[WUS-927] The "Delete" button should be disabled and remark should be displayed in the page S-STU20-01 when the Student Headcount (Secondary) is prepared/confirmed/sent.
</title>
<link>http://helpdesk.hk.ncs-i.com/browse/WUS-927</link>
<description>
The &quot;Delete&quot; button should be disabled and remark should be displayed in the page S-STU20-01 when the Student Headcount (Secondary) is prepared/confirmed/sent. <br/> <br/> The following procedures were conducted to reproduce this problem <br/> 1. Prepare Primary Student HeadCount file. <br/> 2. Prepare Secondary Student HeadCount file. <br/> 3. Unprepare Primary Student HeadCount file.

<item>
<title>
[WUS-821] Processing the incoming E-APP parameter file
</title>
<link>http://helpdesk.hk.ncs-i.com/browse/WUS-821</link>
<description>
For processing the incoming E-APP parameter file: <br/> 1.	The message &quot;File imported successfully.&quot; is missing when a new parameter file is successfully imported. <br/> <br/> School Year <br/> 1.	Error message &quot;Invalid School Year.&quot; should be shown if school year is not in YYYY format. <br/> 2.	Duplicate error message when school year is not an integer and not in YYYY format. <br/> 3.	A redundant error message &quot;數據格式不正確(APLPARM.DAT)&quot; is shown. <br/> <br/> <br/> Submission Period Start Date <br/> 1.	If the start date is not in DD/MM/YYYY format, the parameter file should not be accepted and error message &quot;Invalid Submission Period Start Date.&quot; should be shown. <br/> 2.	If the day or month is not a reasonable integer, the parameter file should not be accepted and error message &quot;Invalid Submission Period Start Date.&quot; should be shown. <br/> 3.	A different error message &quot;匯入參數檔案失敗&quot; is shown if the year of start date is not in YYYY format. Please use the same error message &quot;E-21144: Invalid Submission Period Start Date.&quot; for this scenario. <br/> 4.	The icon should change to if the data file import failed <br/> <br/> Submission Period End Date <br/> 1.	Please refer to the validation rules of submission period start date and the error message should be &quot;Invalid Submission Period End Date.&quot; <br/>
</description>

The access control of the option &quot;Event - Event Offered&quot; should apply to the &quot;Event Offered&quot; tag under &quot;Student Activities &gt; Event &gt; Event Offered &gt; Event Information&quot; instead of the the function &quot;Student Activities &gt; Event &gt; Event Offered&quot;. <br/> <br/> i.e. If user unchecks the option &quot;Event - Event Offered&quot; but selects the option &quot;Event - Event Offered - Student Learning Profile Information&quot;, &quot;Event - Talent Databank (Event) - Add Talent Databank Event&quot; or &quot;Event - Talent Databank (Event) - Add Talent Databank Event Mapping&quot;, the user should be allowed to access the SLP tag or TDB tag under &quot;Event - Event Offered&quot; function. <br/> <br/> <br/> 4.	Please revise the following names of option: <br/> <br/> Eng version: Event - Event Offered - Add Talent Databank Event <br/> Chi version: 課外活動舉辦項目 - 可提供活動項目 - 增新人才資料庫活動項目 <br/> <br/> Eng version: Event - Event Offered - Maintain Talent Databank Event Mapping <br/> Chi version: 課外活動舉辦項目 -可提供活動項目 - 編修人才資料庫活動項目聯繫 <br/> <br/>
</description>

Only 'Left school (Other reason)' requires users to input reasons in 'leave remarks'. <br/> <br/> Thus, the following reason should not require users to input leave remarks: <br/> 'Overseas study' <br/> 'Change school' <br/> 'Emigration' <br/> 'Employment' <br/> 'Deceased' <br/> 'Admitted to Boys'/Girls' Home' <br/> 'Left HK for Mainland/Macau' <br/> 'Reached 15 and left school' <br/> 'Apprentice/VTC/youth program' <br/>
</description>
<environment>UAT103</environment>
<key id="96476">WUS-661</key>
<summary>
Please amend the validation of leave remarks. Only 'Left school (Other reason)' requires users to input reasons in 'leave remarks'.
</summary>
